  • BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. Frequently Asked QuestionsBLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. ntrebri frecvente

    If your the CEO of the supplier company read all the info on our website.Dac suntei administratorul companiei furnizor partener citii toate informaiile de pe website.

    Why does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. needs exclusive rights agreement from supplier partners ?De ce are nevoie BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. contract de distribuie exclusiv de la furnizorii parteneri ?

    Answer: We need the agreement do to fact some clients and competitors try to steal our suppliers, that we work hard to find (it costs time to find good suppliers) Rspuns: Avem nevoie de acest contract fiindc unii clieni i competiia ncearc s ne fure furnizori pentru care am muncit s i gsim. ( cost timp i bani s gseti furnizori buni )

    What is the Declaration of compliance , why does your company CEO needs to sign it ?Ce este Declaraia privind respectarea principiilor, de ce trebuie administratorul companiei furnizor partener s o semneze ?

    Answer: In some countries some people don't respect human and animal rights , environment laws , they put counterfeit products and carcinogenic plastic on the market, they are corrupt. It's a promise your company respects common sense laws and that your a good company. Rspuns: n unele ri oamenii nu respect drepturile omului i ale animalelor, legislaie mediu, pun produse contrafcute i plastic carcinogen pe pia , sunt corupi. Este o promisiune prin care compania declar c respecte legi de bun sim i c este o companie bun cu principii.

    Do i have to pay BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. any money to become a supplier - partner?Cost bani s devii furnizor partner BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. ?

    Answer: NO, we don't take any money from you, the client company pays us commission, you must send us proof you are a legal company and that you have all the documents to add you in our list of suppliers. Rspuns: Nu v costa nimic, dar trebuie s trimitei dovezi c suntei o companie care i desfoar activitatea conform legii i c avei toate documentele pentru a v aduga n lista de furnizori parteneri. Comisionul pentru munca noastr l luam de la companiile clieni, nu de la furnizori parteneri.

    If i am exclusive rights supplier-partner will BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. buy for their clients only from me ?Dac sunt furnizor partener cu contract de distribuie exclusiv BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. va cumpra pentru companiile clieni doar de la mine ?

    Answer: No, we we buy only from supplier-partners that signed the exclusive agreement,in catalog we put supplier-partner with best price, company clients decide what products they want from supplier partners. Rspuns: Nu, noi cumpram ce doresc companiile clieni de la furnizori parteneri care au semnat contract de distribuie exclusiv cu BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. , indiferent c avei cel mai bun pre , este decizia companiei client de la cine cumpr. Noi afiam furnizorul partener cu cel mai bun pre n catalog i restul este decizia companiei client.

    Is it possible to run away with clients 100% advance payment or to scam the clients or suppliers ?Este posibil ca cineva s fug cu avansul de 100% trimis de compania client sau clieni pot fi nelai de furnizori parteneri ?

    Answer: No because the money is traceable, it is all done electronic via bank transfer, it can be easy traced. For large amounts of money, banks request all documents before you can deposit, send or withdraw. There are security measures to prevent bad things. Company bank accounts are not like personal bank accounts or cash. You can use them for company needs only. Rspuns: Nu, fiindc banii sunt trasabil, totul este fcut electronic prin transfer bancar, este uor trasabil. Pentru sume mari de bani, bncile solicit toate documentele nainte de a depozita, transfera sau a de a putea retrage banii din cont. Sunt msuri de securitate implementate de bnci pentru a preveni furturi i nelciuni. Conturile bancare ale companiilor nu sunt asemenea conturilor bancare personale, nu poi s te duci s retragi cum vrei i cnd vrei banii societii. Banii i poi folosi doar pentru nevoile companiei i trebuie s dovedeti asta.

    If i am a supplier - partner can i get my money in cash ?Dac sunt furnizor partener pot primi banii n mn / cash ?

    Answer: No , you will get your money via bank transfer only after client inspects the product(s) on arrival and after he signs over the handover acceptance report. If products are not like in commission contract either transporter did not transport properly the products, you the supplier did not packaged properly the products or the products or not the same we agreed in exclusive rights contract. You will not get payed for damaged products or products that are not the same as in commission contract and exclusive rights agreement. All have to be traced for governments taxes and accounting reasons also. Rspuns: Nu, banii i vei primi doar prin transfer bancar dup ce companiile clieni inspecteaz produsele cnd ajung la destinaie i dup ce companiile clieni semneaz procesul verbal de predare primire. Dac produsele nu sunt la fel ca cele descrise n contractul de comision sau dac sunt ambalate necorespunztor, au defecte sau dac nu sunt la fel cu cele descrise n contractul de distribuie exclusiv, nu vei primi nici un ban. Totul trebuie s fie trasabil pentru ca guvernele s poat lua taxele corect.

    Can i get my money via letter of credit 30% in advance or via other method ?Pot primi banii prin incasso, acreditiv documentar 30% sau n avans sau prin alt metod ?

    Answer: No , the commission contract is standard for all companies. We all get payed after client inspects product when it arrives at his location and after he signs handover acceptance report. BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. just escrows the electronic money for all parties until goods are delivered. Rspuns: Nu, contractul de comision este standard pentru toate companiile. Toi suntem pltii dup ce produsele ajung la locaia companiei client, dup ce le inspecteaz i dup ce semneaz procesul verbal de predare primire. BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. doar ine n escrow banii electronici pentru toate prile pn cnd bunurile sunt livrate.

    Does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. advertise my products ? BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. face reclam produselor mele dac sunt furnizor partener ?

    Answer: No, we advertise BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. like a supermarket but B2B, your product will be in a catalog and people will buy it if they want it. Rspuns: Nu, noi facem reclam doar pentru piaa BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L., ca i cnd ai face reclam unui supermarket B2B ( Angro ), produsele dumneavoasta vor fi n catalog i dac produsele dumneavoasta au cutare, companiile clieni le vor cumpr.

    Does BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. store and transport the products ?BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. depoziteaz i transport produse ?

    Answer: No, we aquire products for client companies only on demand, we store products only if they pay for this service and we hire transporters to transport the goods if client companies pay for this service.
    We don't store products just to have them on stock, and pay bills for things we don't need, we try to lower product(s) prices, buy quality products only on demand for clients and we try to reduce energy costs for us and our clients.     Rspuns: Nu, noi achiziionam produse pentru companii clieni doar la cererea acestora, nu depozitm produse, dect dac companiile client pltesc pentru nchiriere depozite sau cutam i angajam transportatori dac companiile clieni pltesc pentru acest serviciu.
    Noi nu cumpram produse pentru a le ine pe stoc , nu pltim facturi pentru lucruri care nu ne sunt necesare , ncercm s reducem costurile produselor, s cumpram produse de calitate doar la cererea clienilor adic s reducem costurile cu energia pentru noi i companiile clieni.

  • Company Policy Politica Companiei


    a) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. does not export, import, transport or store products for ex communists Romanian "Securitatea" members that did political police, communist political activists, racists, communist torturers or ex legionaries - iron guard or supporters or any other type of extremists; a) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. nu export, nu import, nu depoziteaz produse pentru foti membri ai Securitii care au fcut poliie politic, activiti de partid comuniti, rasiti, torioniti sau ex legionari - garda de fier sau suporteri ai acestora sau pentru alte tipuri de extremiti;

    b) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. does not export, import, transport or store products from armed conflict zones, we do not work with dictators, war criminals, terrorists, corrupt officials and government clerks, criminal enterprises, gangs, cartels and organized crime syndicates; b) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. nu export, nu import, nu depoziteaz produse din zone de conflict militare, nu colaborm cu dictatori, criminali de rzboi, teroriti, politicieni i funcionari corupi, cartel-uri, clanuri interlope, grupri crim organizat;

    c) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. does not export,import,transport or store tobacco, hunting articles, guns, ammo, drinking alcohol, hemp, hemp seeds, plants and mushrooms that are toxic, prohibited substances, drinks, snacks and sweets that contain banned additives or refined sugar; c) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. nu export, nu import i nu transport tutun, articole de vntoare, arme, muniie. produse care conin alcool etilic de but, cnep, semine de cnep, plante i ciuperci toxice-duntoare, substane interzise, buturi, sucuri, snack-uri i dulciuri care conin aditivi alimentari sau zahr rafinat;

    d) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. does not export wood logs or wood products that are not FSC and/or PEFC certified , even if certified you as the supplier company must send proof the products come from sustainable exploitation of forests; d) BLUE SEA EXPORT IMPORT S.R.L. nu export, nu import i nu transport buteni i produse din lemn care nu sunt certificate FSC i/sau PEFC , chiar dac sunt certificate, compania furnizor trebuie s trimit dovezi c produsele provin din exploataii forestiere sustenabile;
